 The central government had asked the states to reduce VAT to reduce the prices of petrol diesel
 nitish kumaar ne kaha ki is base price main barauni rifinary ko jo entry tex lagata he, vah paisa sidhe to le nahin sakate the
 For this reason, he used to take it through all these things
 jiesti aane ke baad yah sab cheez bhi band ho gai he
 Nitish told the central government that by calculating the tax, our base price will also be reduced and we charge those who are on petrol or on diesel
 bihar kaa waite ek-do rajyon se chhodkar adhikansh rajyon se kam hi he, maatr 26 fisad petrol par or 19 fisad dijal par he
 Bihar is already the lowest VAT levying state
 agar base price ghat jayega to apane aap yahaan petrol-dijal kii keemat ghat jaaegi
 Bihar CM Nitish Kumar said that despite all these things, despite telling all the things, we will sit together and discuss and this time not once before there was a big increase in the price of petrol and diesel
 hamane apane rajya main us ko kam kiya tha
 For some time, we are going to consider all those things among ourselves, but we have urged the government to look at the base price once, because in Jharkhand it is 51 rupees, then how did we get 55 rupees
 ek haalia adhyayan kii report main yah khulaasa kiya gaya ki offis jane vaali mahilaon ko aise purushon ke mukaable zyada tanaav hota he, jo offis jate hai
 They also have a greater risk of depression due to more stress than men
 adhyayan kii report main yah bhi daawa kiya gaya ki kariyar main mahilaayein jaise-jaise aage badhati hai unamem depressant kaa khatra utana hi zyada hota chalaa jaataa he
 During research, it was also found that women are more likely to get salary than husband
 is adhyayan ko america kii uniwarsity of ilinois ke shodhakartaaon ne kiya he
 According to the researchers, who is providing the most financial help to the family and it also affects their psychology
 adhyayan main paaya gaya ki apane parivaar ke duusare sadasyon ke muqablemahilaon kii ijise-jaise badhati he, unamem depressant ke lakshan aane lag jate hai
 Researchers Karen Kramer and Sujin Pak found that with the increase in income, men not only improve their standard of living, but also have a positive effect on their mental health
 is adhyayan main 1463 purushon or 1769 mahilaon ko shaamil kiya gaya or unke manovigyaan or maansik sehat kii jaanch kii gai
 The report of the study claimed that when a woman takes care of her children and taking leave for family, she does not have any significant negative effect on her mental health
 lekin iske vipareet purush jababacchon kii dekhbhaal ke lieghar par rukate hai to unki maansik sehat par iskaa asar dekhne ko miltaa he
 Researchers said that during the study, women and men saw a difference in job and household responsibilities and the depression they caused
 bacchon yaa ghar kii dekharekh ke liye kaam chhodane valepurushon main jahaan depressanaka str zyada paaya gaya, vahiin mahilaon ke maansik sehat par iskaa koi khaas asar nahin dekha gaya
 No one has truly forgotten the song sung by Mohammad Rafi, 'tum mujhe yoon bhula na paoge' and no one has forgotten the singer
 vah bhartiya cinema ke aise diggaj gayak the, jinhone apni sureeli geeton se sabakaa man moh liya
 His songs sung are still heard with great fervor
 rafee chah baar sarvshereshth gayak ke rup main filmphere puraskaar se navaaje ja chuke hai
 He is still alive in the hearts of crores of people
 rafee kaa janm 24 disambar, 1924 ko amritsar ke paas kotla sultan singh main hua tha
 When he was younger, his family moved from Lahore to Amritsar
 rafee ke bade bhai kii nai kii dukaan thi
 Rafi used to spend more time there
 us dukaan se hokar ek fakir gaate hue gujara karte the
 Seven-year-old Rafi followed him and kept humming the songs of the fakir
 ek din fakir ne rafee ko gaate hue sun liya
 Impressed by his melodious voice, the fakir blessed Rafi to become a very big singer, which later grew well
 inke bade bhai mohammad hamid ne gayan main inaki dilchaspee ko dekhte hue ustad abdul vaahid khan se shiksha praapt karne kii salaah di
 Once famous singer Kundan Lal Sehgal came to sing the song on the open stage for Akashvani (all India Radio Lahore) but Sehgal refused to sing due to lightning
 logon kaa gussa shant karaane ke liye rafee ke bhai ne aayojakon se rafee ko gane dene kaa anurodh kiya, is tarah 13 saal kii umr main rafee ne pehali baar aamantrit shrotaaon ke saamne prastuti di
 Mohammed Rafi then sang for the Punjabi film Gul Baloch (1944)
 unhone 1946 main mumbai jane kaa faisla kiya
 Music composer Naushad gave him a chance to sing in the film 'pehle Aap'
 naushaad ke sangeet se saji film 'anmol ghadi' (1946) ke geet 'tera khilonaa tutaa' se rafee ko pehali baar prasiddhi mili
 The songs sung by Rafi for 'shaheed', 'mela', and 'dulari' were very popular, but the songs of 'baiju Bawra' made Rafi stand out among the mainstream singers
 naushaad ke liye rafee ne kai geet gaae
 shankar-jaikishan also liked Rafi's songs and also gave Rafi a chance to sing his rhythmic songs
 vah madan mohan, gulam haidar, jayadev jaise sangeet nirdeshkon kii pehali pasand ban gaye
 The songs sung by Rafi starred Dilip Kumar, Bharat Bhushan, Devanand, Shammi Kapoor, Rajesh Khanna, Dharmendra
 'chaudaavin kaa chand' (1960) ke sheershak geet ke liye rafee ko pehali baar film fere puraskaar mila
 In 1961 Rafi received the second Filmfare Award for the song 'teri pyari-pyari Surat' from the film 'sasural'
 sangeetkaar lakshmikant ne filmi duniya main apana aagaaj hi rafee kii madhur aawaaj ke saath kiya
 He won the third Filmfare Award for the song 'chahunga Main Tujhe Saanjh Saver' from the film 'dosti' (1965), adorned with laxmikant-pyarelal tunes
 unhen 1965 main padmashri puraskaar se bhi nawaja gaya
 He received the fourth award for the song 'bahar Phool Barsaon' from the 1966 film Sooraj
 1968 main 'brahmacharee' film ke geet 'dil ke jharokhe main tujko bithakar' ke liye unhen pachvaan filmphere puraskaar mila or 1977 kii film 'ham kisi se kam nahin' ke gane 'kya hua tera vaada' ke liye gayak ko chatha puraskaar mila
 When Rafi was 13 years old, he first married his aunt's daughter Basheran Begum
 rafee ne yah baat chipa rakhi thi
 He took talak from Basheeran after a few years
 iske baad unki duusari shaadi vilkis begum ke saath hui
 Rafi became the father of three sons and four daughters
 unki bahu yasmine khalid rafee ne jab apni kitaab 'mohammad rafee : mere abba (ek sansmaran)' main is mahaan gayak kii pehali shaadi kaa zikr kiya, tab logon ko is bare main pataa chalaa
 Once Rafi had a dispute with Lata Mangeshkar over royalty
 rafee kehete the ki gaanaa gaakar mehtaanaa lene ke baad roylty lene kaa sawaal hi nahin uthta, vahiin lata kahati thim ki gane se hone vaali aamadani kaa hissaa gayak-gayikaon ko jarur milanaa chahie
 There was a feud between the two about this
 donon ne saath gaanaa band kar diya
 Later, at the behest of Nargis, the duo sang the song 'dil Pukare Aa Re a Re a Re' from the film 'jewel Thief'
 ek din achaanak rafee kaa rukhsat ho janaa sabko rulaa gaya
 The great singer probably had a sense of his departure from the world
 31 july, 1980 ko unhone apana gaanaa record karaane ke baad lakshmikant-pyarelal se kaha, "nau ai vil live" or shaam 7
 After leaving the party at 30 o'clock they left us all forever
 jab sangeet ke is betaj badshaah ko supurde khaak kiya ja rahaa tha, to naushaad ye panktiyaan barabas hi budbudane lage- "kahata he koi dil gaya, dilbar chalaa gaya, sahil pukaarata he samandar chalaa gaya, lekin jo baat sach he kahata nahin koi, duniya se mausiki kaa payambar chalaa gaya
 "comments us din hajaaron logon kii ankhen nam thim
 It was raining heavily as if nature was also mourning the departure of this singer
 abhinayta manoj kumaar ne kaha tha ki aisa lagata he ki aaj maa saraswati bhi apane bete ke jane se dukhi hai
 Rafi is not among us today, but his songs are still humming
 rafee ko unke janmdin par shat shat naman!!!(hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he

 ) mohammad rafee ne iske baad punjabi film 'gul baloch' (1944) ke liye gaaya

 Music composer Laxmikant made his debut in the film world with Rafi's melodious voice
 lakshmikant-pyarelal ke dhunon se saji film 'dosti' (1965) ke geet 'chaahunga main tuje sanjh savere' ke liye unhen teesraa filmphere puraskaar mila
 He was also awarded the Padma Shri award in 1965
 1966 kii film 'suraj' ke geet 'bahaaron phool barasaaon' ke liye unhen chauthaa puraskaar mila

 unhone kuch hi saal baad basheeran se taalak le liya

 rafee teen beton or chaar betiyon ke pita bane

 ek baar lata mangeshkar ke saath roylty ko lekar rafee kaa vivaad ho gaya tha
 Rafi used to say that there is no question of taking royalties after singing the song, while Lata used to say that singers and singers must get a share of the income from the song
 ise lekar donon ke bich manmutav ho gaya

 30 baje dal kaa daura padane se ve hameshaa ke liye ham sabko chhodkar chale gaye

 1
 In the first recommendation of the committee, no person can become a BCCI or state association officer after the age of 70 years
 2

 3

 7

 8

 Former judge Markandey Katju said that the public is the highest in a democracy, be it PM or CM
 markandeya katju (markandey Katju) ne twit kar kaha, '' kisi bhi loktantr main janata sabhi athurity se upar he, phir chaahe wo raashtrapati hon, pradhanmantri, mukhyamantri, jaj, vidhayak, beurocret, police, sena ho yaa anya koi
 They are all public servants ''
 markandeya katju (markandey Katju) ne aage likhaa, ''chunki janata master he or jaj unke sevak, isaliye janata thik usee tarah jajon kii bhi aalochana kar sakati he, jis tarah master ko apane naukar kii aalochana kaa adhikaar hota he''
 In a democracy the people are supreme and all authorities, whether President or the Prime Minister, Chief Minister, other ministers, judges, legislators, bureaucrats, police, army and so on are nothing but servants of the people
 aapako bataa den ki pichley dinon hi markandeya katju (markandey Katju) ne supreme court ke ayodhya vivaad ko madhyasthata ke jariye sulajhane ke faisle par chutki lee thi

" isaliye main sirf yahi kah saktaa hum ki- jai ranjan gogoi
 "katju further said in another tweet," Can anyone tell me whether the Supreme Court has ordered mediation or mediation or medicine? i don't understand '' Since the people are the masters and judges their servants, the people have a right to criticize judges just as a master has the right to criticize his servant
 darasal, supreme court (supreme Court)ne madhyasthata ke jariye ayodhya( Ayodhya) menram mandir cese(ram Mandir Case)kaa samaadhaan karne ko kaha he
 The supreme court of the country has appointed a panel of a total of three mediators to resolve the case through dialogue with both the parties
